jane goodall helps humans and animals live together	珍妮亞爾能協助人類和動物一起生活 。
good afternoon , good evening , whatever .	晚安 , 晚安 , 不管如何 。
we can go , jambo , guten abend , bonsoir , but we can also ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh .	我們可以去 , 喔 , 喔 , ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~
that is the call that chimpanzees make before they go to sleep in the evening .	這就是黑猩猩在晚上睡前所謂的 「 黑猩猩 」 。
you hear it going from one side of the valley to the other , from one group of nests to the next .	你聽到它從山谷的一邊到另一邊 , 從一群巢穴到下一個 。
and i want to pick up with my talk this evening from where zeray left off yesterday .	我想從昨天離開的地方挑起我的演講 。
he was talking about this amazing , threeyearold australopithecine child , selam .	他在談論這個驚人的 , 三歲的澳洲兒童 , 塞拉姆 。
and we've also been hearing about the history , the family tree , of mankind through dna genetic profiling .	我們也聽過歷史 , 家庭樹 , 由dna複製出來的人類 。
and it was a paleontologist , the late louis leakey , who actually set me on the path for studying chimpanzees .	那是一名古生物學家 , 最近的路易斯•李迪 , 他把我放在研究黑猩猩的路上 。
and it was pretty extraordinary , way back then .	那時很不尋常 , 回到那兒 。
it's kind of commonplace now , but his argument was because he'd been searching for the fossilized remains of early humans in africa .	這有點常見 , 但他的論點是因為他一直在尋找非洲早期人類的化石 。
and you can tell an awful lot about what those beings looked like from the fossils , from the shape of the muscle attachments , something about the way they lived from the various artifacts found with them .	你可以告訴那些從化石的形狀 , 從肌肉的形狀 , 從肌肉的形狀 , 到他們生活的方式 , 和他們所發現的各種人物相處 。
but what about how they behaved ? that's what he wanted to know .	但他們是怎麼樣的 ? 那是他想知道的 。
and of course , behavior doesn't fossilize .	當然 , 行為不會化石 。
he argued and it's now a fairly common theory that if we found behavior patterns similar or the same in our closest living relatives , the great apes , and humans today , then maybe those behaviors were present in the apelike , humanlike ancestor some seven million years ago .	他爭論了 , 現在是一個很常見的理論 , 如果我們找到了行為模式 , 或在我們最接近的居住人的親戚、人類的同性戀 , 或許這些行為在彼得時出現 , 人類的祖先在某七百萬年前 。
and therefore , perhaps we had brought those characteristics with us from that ancient , ancient past .	因此 , 或許我們把這些特徵帶給我們 , 從古老、古老的過去 。
well , if you look in textbooks today that deal with human evolution , you very often find people speculating about how early humans may have behaved , based on the behavior of chimpanzees .	嗯 , 如果你今天看教科書來處理人類進化 , 你通常會發現人們在說早期人類的行為 , 可能是基於黑猩猩的行為 。
they are more like us than any other living creature , and we've heard about that during this ted conference .	他們比其他生物還像我們一樣 , 我們在ted會議中聽過這一點 。
so it remains for me to comment on the ways in which chimpanzees are so like us , in certain aspects of their behavior .	所以 , 我一直在評論黑猩猩的方式 , 像我們一樣 , 在某些方面 , 我們的行為中 。
every chimpanzee has his or her own personality .	每隻黑猩猩都有自己的性格 。
of course , i gave them names . they can live to be 60 years or more , although we think most of them probably don't make it to 60 in the wild .	當然 , 我給了他們名字 。 他們可以活60年或更多 , 雖然我們認為大部分人可能不會在野外製造到60個 。
mr . wurzel . the female has her first baby when she's 11 or 12 .	當她11或12歲時 , 雌性就有她第一個嬰兒 。
thereafter , she has one baby only every five or six years , a long period of childhood dependency when the child is nursing , sleeping with the mother at night , and riding on her back .	在那裡 , 她每五到六年 , 只有一個嬰兒 , 長期的童年被養育 , 當孩子們在晚上睡覺 , 睡在她背後 。
and we believe that this long period of childhood is important for chimpanzees , just as it is for us , in relation to learning .	我們相信這種長期的童年對黑猩猩來說很重要 , 就如同我們一樣 , 學習的關係 。
as the brain becomes ever more complex during evolution in different forms of animals , so we find that learning plays an ever more important role in an individual's life history .	當大腦在不同類型的動物演化過程中變得更複雜 , 所以我們發現學習在個人生命歷史上扮演著更重要的角色 。
and young chimpanzees spend a lot of time watching what their elders do .	年輕的黑猩猩花了很多時間去看他們的老人做些什麼 。
we know now that they're capable of imitating behaviors that they see .	我們現在知道他們可以模仿他們所看到的行為 。
and we believe that it's in this way that the different toolusing behaviors that have now been seen in all the different chimpanzee populations studied in africa how these are passed from one generation to the next , through observation , imitation and practice , so that we can describe these toolusing behaviors as primitive culture .	我們相信 , 以這種方式描述不同的工具行為 , 在非洲各式各樣的黑猩猩群中 , 研究這些是如何從一個世代傳遞到下一代 , 透過觀察 , 模仿和練習 , 這樣我們就能描述這些突破的行為 , 作為原始文化 。
chimpanzees don't have a spoken language . we've talked about that .	黑猩猩沒有語言 , 我們談過這一點 。
they do have a very rich repertoire of postures and gestures , many of which are similar , or even identical , to ours and formed in the same context . greeting chimpanzees embracing .	他們的確有非常豐富的姿勢和姿勢 , 許多都是相似的 , 甚至相同的 , 在同一個情境中形成 , 希臘黑猩猩會擁抱 。
they also kiss , hold hands , pat one another on the back .	他們也吻了 , 握住手 , 另一隻手 。
and they swagger and they throw rocks .	牠們會游泳 , 扔石頭 。
in chimpanzee society , we find many , many examples of compassion , precursors to love and true altruism .	在黑猩猩社會中 , 我們發現許多同情的例子 , 包括愛和真實的利他主義 。
unfortunately , they , like us , have a dark side to their nature .	不幸的是 , 他們像我們一樣 , 有黑暗的一面 。
they're capable of extreme brutality , even a kind of primitive war .	他們有極端的殘酷性 , 甚至是一種原始的戰爭 。
and these really aggressive behaviors , for the most part , are directed against individuals of the neighboring social group .	這些真的很具侵略性的行為 , 最多部分是對鄰近社會團體的個人有歧視 。
they are very territorially aggressive .	他們是非常有侵略力的 。
chimpanzees , i believe , more than any other living creature , have helped us to understand that , after all , there is no sharp line between humans and the rest of the animal kingdom .	我相信 , 黑猩猩 , 我相信 , 比其他生物還能幫助我們了解 , 畢竟 , 人類和其他動物王國之間沒有鯊魚線 。
it's a very blurry line , and it's getting more blurry all the time as we make even more observations .	它是一條非常模糊的線 , 每當我們製造更多的觀察時 , 就會變得越來越模糊 。
the study that i began in 1960 is still continuing to this day .	我從1960年開始的研究仍然持續到今日 。
and these chimpanzees , living their complex social lives in the wild , have helped more than anything else to make us realize we are part of , and not separated from , the amazing animals with whom we share the planet .	這些黑猩猩 , 住在野生的複雜社會生活中 , 比其他東西都能幫助我們了解我們是其中的一部分 , 而不是我們共享地球的神奇動物 。
so it's pretty sad to find that chimpanzees , like so many other creatures around the world , are losing their habitats .	所以很難找到黑猩猩 , 就像世界上許多其他生物一樣 , 都失去了棲息地 。
this is just one photograph from the air , and it shows you the forested highlands of gombe .	這只是從空氣中拍攝的照片 , 它給你們看了木林高地的高地 。
and it was when i flew over the whole area , about 16 years ago , and realized that outside the park , this forest , which in 1960 had stretched almost unbroken along the eastern shore of lake tanganyika , which is where the tiny , 30squaremile gombe national park lies , that a question came to my mind .	大約16年前 , 我飛過整個區域 , 發現在公園外面的森林 , 1960年 , 在湖岸沿著湖岸的東岸 , 也就是小型的三十平方公園公園 , 一個問題出現在我腦海外 。
" how can we even try to save these famous chimpanzees , when the people living around the national park are struggling to survive ? "	「 我們要如何拯救這些有名的黑猩猩 , 當國家公園裡的人在掙扎生存時 , 我們要如何拯救這些有名的黑猩猩 ? 」
more people are living there than the land could possibly support .	更多人住在那裡 , 比土地還能支持 。
the numbers increased by refugees pouring in from burundi and over the lake from congo .	難民的數量增加 , 來自地獄和剛果湖泊的湖泊 。
and very poor people they couldn't afford to buy food from elsewhere .	非常貧窮的人 , 他們無法從其他地方買食物 。
this led to a program , which we call tacare .	這導致了一項計畫 , 我們稱之為tacare 。
it's a very holistic way of improving the lives of the people living in the villages around the park .	這是個非常嚴格的改善人們生活在村莊裡的生活方式 。
it started small with 12 villages . it's now in 24 .	它從12個村落開始 , 現在是24年 。
there isn't time to go into it , but it's including things like tree nurseries , methods of farming most suitable to this now very degraded , almost desertlike land up in these mountains .	沒有時候要走進去 , 但它包含了樹木護士 , 農場最適合的農場 , 幾乎是沙漠在這些山上降落 。
ways of controlling , preventing soil erosion .	控制方式 , 防止土壤排放 。
ways of reclaiming overused farmland , so that within two years they can again be productive .	重複過度農地的方式 , 所以在兩年內 , 他們能再次成為生產力 。
working to help the villagers obtain fresh water from wells .	努力協助村民從好處取得淡水 。
perhaps build some schoolrooms .	也許建造一些學校 。
most important of all , i believe , is working with small groups of women , providing them with opportunities for microcredit loans .	最重要的是 , 我相信 , 與少數女性合作 , 提供他們對微型credit貸款的機會 。
and we've got , as is the case around the world , about 95 percent of all loans returned .	我們有 , 就像全世界的案例 , 大約有95%的貸款 。
empowering women , working with education , providing scholarships for girls so they can finish secondary school , in the clear understanding that , all around the world , as women's education improves , family size drops .	賦予女性 , 和教育合作 , 為女孩提供獎學金 , 讓他們能完成第二級學校 , 清楚地了解到 , 身為婦女教育改善 , 家庭大小 。
we provide information about family planning and about hiv/aids .	我們提供關於家庭規劃和愛滋病的資訊 。
and as a result of this program , something's happening for conservation .	作為這個計畫的結果 , 保育會發生什麼事 。
what's happening for conservation is that the farmers living in these 24 villages , instead of looking on us as a bunch of white people coming to study a whole bunch of monkeys and by the way , many of the staff are now tanzanian but when we began the tacare program , it was a tanzanian team going into the villages .	保育的情況是 , 農夫生活在24個村莊裡 , 而不是把我們當作一群白人人來研究一大堆猴子 , 順便說一提 , 很多人現在是坦尚尼亞人 , 但當我們開始計劃時 , 它是坦尚尼亞的團隊 。
it was a tanzanian team talking to the villagers , asking what they were interested in .	那是坦尚尼亞的團隊和村民談話 , 問他們對什麼 。
were they interested in conservation ? absolutely not .	他們對保育有興趣嗎 ? 絕對不是 。
they were interested in health ; they were interested in education .	他們對健康有興趣 , 他們對教育有興趣 。
and as time went on , and as their situation began to improve , they began to understand ever more about the need for conservation .	隨著時間進步 , 隨著他們的情況開始改善 , 他們開始更了解保育的需求 。
they began to understand that as the upper levels of the hills were denuded of trees , so you've got this terrible soil erosion and mudslides .	他們開始了解 , 身為山丘的上層層面 , 所以你有很糟糕的土壤排放和泥土 。
today , we are developing what we call the greater gombe ecosystem .	現今 , 我們正在發展出我們所謂的 「 高爾蒙生態系統 」 。
this is an area way outside the national park , stretching out into all these very degraded lands .	這是國家公園外的一個地方 , 伸出這些非常乾燥的土地 。
and as these villages have a better standard of life , they are actually agreeing to put between 10 percent and 20 percent of their land in the highlands aside , so that once again , as the trees grow back , the chimpanzees will have leafy corridors through which they can travel to interact as they must for genetic viability with other remnant groups outside the national park .	隨著這些村落有更好的生命標準 , 他們其實同意在高地的百分之十到二十的土地中 , 再一次 , 隨著樹木長回來 , 黑猩猩會穿透透鏡 , 牠們可以與其它的基因互動 。
so tacare is a success .	所以tacare是成功的 。
we're replicating it in other parts of africa , around other wilderness areas which are faced with extreme population pressure .	我們在非洲其他地方複製它 , 在其他地方 , 和其他荒野地區 , 面對極端人口壓力 。
the problems in africa , however , as we've been discussing for the whole of these first couple of days of ted , are major problems .	然而 , 非洲的問題 , 隨著我們在討論ted的前幾天 , ted是主要的問題 。
there is a great deal of poverty .	有許多貧窮 。
and when you get large numbers of people living in land that is not that fertile , particularly when you cut down trees , and you leave the soil open to the wind for erosion , as desperate populations cut down more and more trees , so that they can try and grow food for themselves and their families , what's going to happen ? something's got to give .	當你有大量的居民住在土地裡 , 特別是當你切下樹 , 你就把土壤打開 , 把土壤砍掉 , 把更多的樹木砍掉 , 這樣他們就可以為自己種植食物 , 什麼會發生 ?
and the other problems in not only africa , but the rest of the developing world and , indeed , everywhere what are we doing to our planet ?	另外一個問題不只是非洲 , 而是其他發展中國家的其他問題 , 確實 , 我們在地球上做的事 ?
you know , the famous scientist , e . o . wilson said that if every person on this planet attains the standard of living of the average european or american , we need three new planets .	你知道的 , 那些有名的科學家 , e.o.wilson說 , 如果地球上的每個人都住在一般歐洲或美國 , 我們需要三個新的行星 。
today , they are saying four . but we don't have them . we've got one .	現今 , 他們說了四個 , 但我們沒有 。 我們有一個 。
and what's happened ? i mean , the question here is , here we are , arguably the most intelligent being that's ever walked planet earth , with this extraordinary brain , capable of the kind of technology that is so well illustrated by these ted conferences , and yet we're destroying the only home we have .	發生了什麼事 ? 我的意思是 , 這裡的問題是 , 我們是說 , 最聰明的是走過地球上最有智慧的大腦 , 有著這種非凡的大腦 , 能夠被ted會議所描述的科技 , 但我們還在摧毀我們唯一的家 。
the indigenous people around the world , before they made a major decision , used to sit around and ask themselves , " how does this decision affect our people seven generations ahead ? "	世界各地的原住民 , 在他們做了重大決策之前 , 常常坐下來問自己: 「 這決定如何影響我們七世代的人 ? 」
today , major decisions and i'm not particularly talking about africa here , but the developed world major decisions involving millions of dollars , and millions of people , are often based on , " how will this affect the next shareholders' meeting ? "	今天 , 主要的決策 , 我不特別在談論非洲 , 但在發展中國家的主要決策是數百萬美元 , 而數百萬人通常是基於 「 這會如何影響下一個共享者的會議 ? 」
and these decisions affect africa .	這些決策會影響非洲 。
as i began traveling around africa talking about the problems faced by chimpanzees and their vanishing forests , i realized more and more how so many of africa's problems could be laid at the door of previous colonial exploitation .	當我在非洲各地旅行時 , 談到黑猩猩和他們的消費森林面臨的問題時 , 我了解到更多的非洲的問題 , 可能在之前的殖民部門被推進 。
so i began traveling outside africa , talking in europe , talking in the united states , going to asia .	所以 , 我開始在非洲旅行 , 在歐洲談話 , 在美國 , 去亞洲 。
and everywhere there were these terrible problems .	到處都有這些可怕的問題 。
and you know the kind i'm talking about . i'm talking about pollution .	各位知道我在說的 , 我說的是污染 。
the air that we breathe that often poisons us .	我們呼吸的空氣通常會毒我們 。
the earth is poisoning our foods .	地球在毒害我們的食物 。
the water water is perhaps one of the most crucial issues that we're going to face in this century and everywhere water is being polluted by agricultural , industrial and household chemicals that still are being sprayed around the world , seemingly with the inability to profit from past experience .	水可能是我們在這個世紀中所面對的最關鍵問題之一 , 到處都被農業、工業和家庭化學物質所污染 , 仍然被世界各地散播 , 似乎和過去的經驗中 , 似乎是無法獲利的 。
the mangroves are being cut down ; the effects of things like the tsunami get worse .	紅樹枝被切割 ; 像海嘯的影響會更糟 。
we've talked about the soil erosion .	我們談到土壤排放 。
we have the reckless burning of fossil fuels along with other greenhouse gasses , so called , leading to climate change .	我們和其他溫室氣體一樣有無比的燃料 , 叫做 「 氣候變遷 」 。
finally , all around the world , people have begun to believe that there is something going on very wrong with our climate .	最後 , 世界各地 , 人們開始相信 , 我們的氣候發生了很大的錯誤 。
all around the world climates are mixed up .	世界各地的氣候都混合起來 。
and it's the poor people who are affected worse .	最貧窮的人會更糟糕 。
it's africa that already is affected .	非洲已經受到影響 。
in many parts of subsaharan africa , the droughts are so much worse .	在撒哈拉以南非洲的許多地區 , 乾旱很糟 。
and when the rain does come , it so often leads to flooding and added distress , and the cycle of poverty and hunger and disease .	當雨林來臨時 , 通常會導致洪水、加入的災難 , 以及貧窮、飢餓和疾病的循環 。
and the numbers of people living in an area that the land cannot support , who are too poor to buy food , who can't move away because the whole land is degraded .	而住在一個地方的人數無法支持 , 他們太貧窮買食物 , 因為整個土地已經退化了 。
and so you get desertification creeping , creeping , creeping as the last of the trees are cut down .	所以你會得到沙漠化、哭泣 , 直到最後一棵樹被砍掉 。
and this kind of thing is not just in africa . it's all over the world .	這種事情不僅在非洲 , 都在全世界 。
so it wasn't surprising to me that as i was traveling around the world i met so many young people who seemed to have lost hope .	所以 , 我驚訝的是 , 當我在世界各地旅行時 , 我遇到許多年輕人似乎失去了希望 。
we seem to have lost wisdom , the wisdom of the indigenous people .	我們似乎失去智慧 , 原住民的智慧 。
i asked a question . " why ? "	我問一個問題: 「 為什麼 ? 」
well , do you think there could be some kind of disconnect between this extraordinarily clever brain , the kind of brain that the ted technologies exemplify , and the human heart ? talking about it in the nonscientific term , in terms of love and compassion . is there some disconnect ?	嗯 , 你認為 , 可能有某種不同的大腦之間的區別 , ted的科技擴大了 , 人類的心臟 ? 談到它 , 在非科學方面 , 在愛和同情方面 , 是否有一些區別 ?
and these young people , when i talk to them , basically they were either depressed or apathetic , or bitter and angry . and they said more or less the same thing , " we feel this way because we feel you've compromised our future and there's nothing we can do about it . "	而這些年輕人 , 當我和他們談話時 , 基本上 , 他們是憂鬱或痛苦 , 或憤怒 。 他們說了更多或少說同樣的事 , 因為我們覺得你覺得你對未來的抱怨 , 沒有任何我們能做的事 。 」
we have compromised their future .	我們已經承認了他們的未來 。
i've got three little grandchildren , and every time i look at them and i think how we've harmed this beautiful planet since i was their age , i feel this desperation .	我有三個小孫子 , 每當我看著他們時 , 我想我們如何傷害這個美麗的星球 , 我覺得這個絕望 。
and that led to this program we call roots and shoots , which began right here in tanzania and has now spread to 97 countries around the world .	這個計畫導致了我們稱之為根和射擊 , 開始在坦尚尼亞 , 現在已經擴散到全世界97個國家 。
it's symbolic . roots make a firm foundation .	它是象徵性的 。 樹根製造了一間公司基金會 。
shoots seem tiny ; to reach the sun they can break through a brick wall .	射擊看起來很小 , 去到它們能穿過磚牆的太陽 。
see the brick wall as all these problems we've inflicted on the planet , environmental and social . it's a message of hope .	把磚牆當作我們在地球上所帶來的所有問題 , 環保和社交 。 這是希望的訊息 。
hundreds and thousands of young people around the world can break through and can make this a better world for all living things .	全世界有數以千計的年輕人可以打破 , 讓這世界變得更好 。
the most important message of roots and shoots: every single one of us makes a difference , every single day .	最重要的訊息是根和槍擊:我們每個人每一天都有不同的差異 。
we have a choice . every one of us in this room , we have a choice as to what kind of difference we want to make .	我們有選擇 。 在這房間裡的每一個人 , 我們都有選擇 , 我們想要做些什麼樣的差異 。
the very poor have no choice . it's up to us to change things so that the poor have choice as well .	窮人沒有選擇 , 我們就要改變事情 , 這樣貧窮的選擇也一樣 。
the roots and shoots groups all choose three projects .	根和槍擊團體都選擇了三項計畫 。
it depends on how old they are , and which country , whether they're in a city or rural , as to what kinds of projects .	它依賴了多少年紀 , 而哪個國家 , 不管是城市或鄉村 , 都市 。
but basically , we have programs now from preschool right through university , with more and more adults starting their own roots and shoots groups .	但基本上 , 我們已經從大學學院開始 , 有更多成年人開始自己的根和槍擊團體 。
and every group chooses , between them , three different kinds of project to make this a better world , recognizing that all these different problems are interconnected and impinge on each other .	每個團體選擇 , 在它們之間 , 三種不同的項目 , 來讓這個世界變得更好 , 意識到 , 這些不同的問題都互相連結 , 互相互連結 。
so one of their projects will be to help their own human community .	其中一個專案會幫助自己的人類社群 。
and then , if they're able , they may raise money to help communities in other parts of the world .	然後 , 如果他們能做到 , 他們可能會在世界上其他地方提高資金來幫助社區 。
one of their projects will be to help animals not just wildlife , domestic animals as well .	其中一個計畫 , 協助動物不僅僅是野生動物 , 家庭動物也是 。
and one of their projects will be to help the environment that we all share .	其中一個計畫將會協助我們共享的環境 。
and woven throughout all of this is a message of learning to live in peace and harmony within ourselves , in our families , in our communities , between nations , between cultures , between religions and between us and the natural world .	所有這一切都是學習的訊息 , 在我們家中生活在和平和諧 , 在我們的社區中 , 在我們的社區之間 , 文化之間 , 文化和我們之間的宗教和自然世界之間 。
we need the natural world . we cannot go on destroying it at the rate we are .	我們需要自然的世界 , 我們不能在我們所處的速度下摧毀它 。
we not do have more than this one planet .	我們沒有超過這個星球 。
just picking one or two of the projects right here in africa that the roots and shoots groups are doing , one or two projects only in tanzania , in uganda , kenya , south africa , congobrazzaville , sierra leone , cameroon and other groups . and as i say , it's in 97 countries around the world .	只是在非洲選一或兩項專案計畫 , 非洲的根和槍擊團體正在做 , 一、兩項專案只在坦尚尼亞、肯亞、南非、南非、西班牙、西班牙、相機和其他團體 。 如我所說的 , 在全世界97個國家 。
of course , they're planting trees . they're growing organic vegetables .	當然 , 它們正在種植樹 , 它們正在種植有機蔬菜 。
they're working in the refugee camps , with chickens and selling the eggs for a little amount of money , or just using them to feed their families , and feeling a sense of pride and empowerment , because they're no longer helpless and depending on others with their vegetables and their chickens .	他們在難民營工作 , 有雞蛋 , 賣蛋 , 或用小錢來餵養他們的家人 , 感覺自己是驕傲和權力 , 因為他們不再有幫助 , 依靠蔬菜和雞 。
it's being used in uganda to give some psychological help to exchild soldiers .	它被用在烏干達 , 給予一些心理幫助 , 讓士兵出生 。
doing projects like this is bringing them out of themselves .	做像這樣的專案 , 就是把它們從自己中取出來 。
once again , they're useful members of society .	再一次 , 他們是社會有用的成員 。
we have this program in prisons as well .	我們在監獄裡也有這個計畫 。
so , there's no time for more roots and shoots now .	所以 , 現在沒有更多的根和槍擊時間 。
but oh , they're also working on hiv/aids .	但 , 喔 , 他們也在研究愛滋病 。
that's a very important component of roots and shoots , with older kids talking to younger ones .	這是根和槍擊的重要元素 , 長大的孩子和年輕的孩子談話 。
and unwanted pregnancies and things like that , which young people listen to better from other youth , rather than adults .	沒有預防的懷孕和類似的事情 , 年輕人會傾聽其他年輕人 , 而不是成人 。
hope . that's the question i get asked as i'm going around the world: " jane , you've seen so many terrible things , you've seen your chimpanzees decrease in number from about one million , at the turn of the century , to no more than 150 , 000 now , and the same with so many other animals .	希望 。 這是我在世界各地問的問題: 「 珍 , 你見過太多可怕的事情 , 你看到你的黑猩猩從一個世紀開始 , 開始 , 沒有超過150萬隻 , 和其他其他動物一樣 。
forests disappearing , deserts where once there was forest .	森林消失 , 沙漠一旦有森林 。
do you really have hope ? " well , yes .	你真的有希望嗎 ? " 是的 。
you can't come to a conference like ted and not have hope , can you ?	你不能像ted這樣的會議 , 沒有希望 , 對吧 ?
and of course , there's hope . one is this amazing human brain .	當然 , 有希望 。 一個是令人驚嘆的人類腦 。
and i mean , think of the technologies .	我的意思是 , 想想科技 。
and i've just been so thrilled , finally , to come to people talking about compost latrines .	最後 , 我一直很驚訝 , 最後 , 來到人們談論 「 妥協 」 的演講 。
it's one of my hobbyhorses .	這是我最討厭的其中之一 。
we just flush all this water down the lavatory , it's terrible .	我們只是把這些水流到電梯下面 , 很可怕 。
and then talking about renewable energy desperately important .	接著 , 談到再生能源非常重要 。
do we care about the planet for our children ?	我們是否在乎我們的孩子嗎 ?
how many of us have children or grandchildren , nieces , nephews ?	有多少人有孩子或孫子、姪女、姪女 ?
do we care about their future ?	我們是否在乎他們的未來嗎 ?
and if we care about their future , we , as the elite around the world , we can do something about it . we can make choices as to how we live each day .	如果我們關心他們的未來 , 我們 , 身為世界菁英 , 我們可以做點什麼 。 我們可以把選擇做為我們每天的生活 。
what we buy . what we wear .	我們買了什麼 , 我們穿什麼衣服 。
and choose to make these choices with the question , how will this affect the environment around me ?	選擇做出這些選擇 , 要怎麼影響我周遭的環境 ?
how will it affect the life of my child when he or she grows up ?	當他長大後 , 它會如何影響我的孩子的生活 ?
or my grandchild , or whatever it is .	或是我的孫子 , 或任何東西 。
so the human brain , coupled with the human heart , and we join hands around the world .	所以 , 人類的大腦 , 與人類的心 , 我們加入世界各地的手 。
and that's what ted is helping so well with , and google who help us , and esri are helping us with mapping in gombe national park .	這就是ted的幫助 , 和谷歌幫助我們 , 他們幫助我們 , esri正在幫助我們 , 國民公園的繪製 。
all of these technologies we can use .	所有我們能使用的技術 。
now let's link them , and it's beginning to happen , isn't it ?	現在讓我們連結它們 , 開始發生 , 不是嗎 ?
you've heard about it this afternoon . it's beginning to happen .	你已經聽過這個下午 , 開始發生 。
this change , this change . to see change that we must have if we care about the future .	這種改變 , 要看到改變 , 如果我們關心未來 。
and the next reason for hope nature is amazingly resilient .	希望大自然的下一個原因是非常的韌性 。
you can take an area that's absolutely destroyed , with time and perhaps some help it can regenerate .	你可以拿一塊絕對摧毀的區域 , 有時間 , 或許有些幫助它能再生 。
and an example is the tacare program .	一個例子是 「 計劃計畫 」 。
i told you , where a seemingly dead tree stump if you stop hacking them for firewood , which you don't need to because you have wood lots , then in five years you can have a 30foot tree .	我告訴你們 , 看似死的樹木 , 如果你停止駭客火災 , 那你不需要因為你有木材 , 五年後 , 你可以有三十英尺的樹木 。
and animals , almost on the brink of extinction , can be given a second chance . that's my next book .	動物 , 幾乎在滅絕的橋上 , 可能有第二次機會 。 這是我的下一本書 。
it's inspiring . and it brings me to my last category of hope , and we've heard about this so much in the last two days: this indomitable human spirit . this determination of people , the resilience of the human spirit , so that people who you would think would be battered by poverty , or disease , or whatever , can pull themselves up out of it , sometimes with a helping hand , and take their part in society , and take their part in changing the world .	很鼓舞人心 , 這讓我帶到我最後一類的希望 , 我們在過去兩天都聽過這種現象:這種無限的人類精神 。 人類的精神 , 人類精神的韌性 , 這樣你會認為你會被貧窮、疾病、疾病 , 或疾病 , 或任何東西 , 可以把自己推出去 , 有時 , 把他們自己推出去 , 改變世界 。
and just to think of one or two people out of africa who are just really inspiring .	想想非洲只有一到兩個人 , 他們真的很鼓舞人心 。
we could make a very long list , but obviously nelson mandela , emerging from 17 years of hard physical labor , 23 years of imprisonment , with this amazing ability to forgive , so that he could lead his nation out the evil regime of apartheid without a bloodbath .	我們能製造一個很長的清單 , 但顯然是nelson曼德拉 , 從17年的硬實勞工中出現 , 23年的監禁 , 讓他能引導他的國家 , 避免血液的邪惡政權 。
ken sarowiwa , in nigeria , who took on the giant oil companies , and although people around the world tried their best , was executed .	在奈及利亞 , kensarowiwa , 他在巨大的石油公司 , 雖然世界各地的人都試過最好的 , 被執行了 。
people like this are so inspirational .	像這樣的人如此靈感 。
people like this are the role models we need for young africans .	像這樣的人 , 我們對年輕非洲人所需要的榜樣 。
and we need some environmental role models as well , and i've been hearing some of them today .	我們也需要一些環保的模型 , 我今天聽到了其中一些 。
so i'm really grateful for this opportunity to share this message again , with everyone at ted .	所以 , 我非常感謝這個機會再次分享這個訊息 , 和ted的所有人 。
and i hope that some of us can get together and talk about some of these things , especially the roots and shoots program .	我希望有些人可以一起討論這些事情 , 特別是根和射擊計畫 。
and just a last word on that the young woman who's running this entire conference center , i met her today .	最後一個字 , 那些在進行這整個會議中心的年輕女士 , 我今天見到她 。
she came up so excited , with her certificate . she was [in] roots and shoots .	她很興奮 , 和她的證據很興奮 。 她是根和槍擊 。
she was in the leadership in dar es salaam .	她在達爾薩拉克的領導人中 。
she said it's helped her to do what she's doing .	她說這是幫助她做她做的事 。
and it was very , very exciting for me to meet her and see just one example of how young people , when they are empowered , given the opportunity to take action , to make the world a better place , truly are our hope for tomorrow .	對我來說 , 非常令人興奮 , 看看年輕人的一個例子 , 給予行動的機會 , 讓世界變得更好 , 真正是我們未來的希望 。
artist dianna cohen shares some tough truths about plastic pollution in the ocean and in our lives and some thoughts on how to free ourselves from the plastic gyre .	藝術家dannacohen分享了一些艱難的真相 , 關於海洋中的塑膠污染 , 以及我們生活中的一些思想 , 如何免費塑膠灣 。
consumerism , global issues , green , mission blue , oceans , plastic	消費者、全球議題、綠色、任務藍、海洋、塑膠、塑膠、塑膠、塑膠 , 以及全球性的議題 。
dianna cohen: tough truths about plastic pollution	dannacohen:關於塑膠污染的艱難真相 。
i'm a visual artist , and i'm also one of the cofounders of the plastic pollution coalition .	我是視覺藝術家 , 我也是塑膠污染聯盟的共同創辦人之一 。
i've been working with plastic bags , which i cut up and sew back together as my primary material for my artwork for the last 20 years .	我和塑膠袋合作 , 我把我最初的材料分解為過去20年的藝術作品 。
i turn them into two and threedimensional pieces and sculptures and installations .	我把它們變成兩個三維的作品 , 雕塑和裝置 。
upon working with the plastic , after about the first eight years , some of my work started to fissure and break down into smaller little bits of plastic .	一開始有塑膠 , 大約八年後 , 我有些工作開始累積 , 分成小小的塑膠 。
and i thought , " great .	我心想: 「 太棒了 。
it's ephemeral just like us . "	它就像我們一樣 。 」
upon educating myself a little further about plastics , i actually realized this was a bad thing .	教育自己更遠的是塑膠 , 我真的意識到這是件壞事 。
it's a bad thing that plastic breaks down into smaller little bits , because it's always still plastic .	塑膠會分解成小小的小點 , 因為它總是塑膠 。
and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們所發現的是 , 在海洋環境中 , 大部份都是如此 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	在過去幾年 , 我學到了太平洋的垃圾場和gyre 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	我最初的反應 , 我認為 , 很多人的第一個反應是: 「 天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們必須走出去 , 清理這個東西 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	所以 , 我真的開發了一個建議 , 用一艘卡哥船和兩組的捕魚垃圾機 , 一台車 , 一台船 , 和一台寒冷的機器 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	我的意圖是 , 要走向gyre , 提高這個議題 , 開始採取塑膠 , 把塑膠變成小小的模塊 , 將它當作可在下載社區中所使用的建築材料 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始和當時在海軍環境裡的人談話 , 研究海洋環境裡的塑膠問題 , 這樣做 , 我意識到 , 把它清理成一個非常小的一滴 , 對於全世界的每一天 , 產生了多少 , 其實我需要回頭看更大的照片 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的圖片是:我們需要找到一個方法 , 來阻止它 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要把單一的塑膠分開 , 每天都進入海洋環境 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	因此 , 我也了解到我真的很生氣 。
i wasn't just concerned about plastic that you're trying to imagine out in the middle of the pacific ocean of which i have learned there are now 11 gyres , potentially , of plastic in five major oceans in the world .	我不只關心塑膠你試圖想像在太平洋中間的太平洋中間有11個gres , 可能是世界上五大海裡的塑膠 。
it's not just that gyre of plastic that i'm concerned about it's the gyre of plastic in the supermarket .	這不只是我關心的塑膠 , 而是超級市場的塑膠 。
i'd go to the supermarket and all of my food is packaged in plastic .	我會去超市 , 所有的食物都被包裝在塑膠裡 。
all of my beverages are packaged in plastic , even at the health food market .	所有我在塑膠裡包裝的 , 即使在健康食物市場 。
i'm also concerned about the plastic in the refrigerator , and i'm concerned about the plastic and the toxins that leach from plastic into us and into our bodies .	我也關心冰箱裡的塑膠 , 我擔心塑膠和塑膠的毒素 , 從塑膠到我們體內 , 進入我們的身體 。
so i came together with a group of other people who were all looking at this issue , and we created the plastic pollution coalition .	所以我和一群人一起研究這個議題 , 我們創造了塑膠污染聯盟 。
we have many initiatives that we're working on , but some of them are very basic .	我們有許多我們正在努力的倡議 , 但其中一些是非常基本的 。
one is: if 80 to 90 percent of what we're finding in the ocean of the marine debris that we're finding in the ocean is plastic , then why don't we call it what it is .	第一:如果我們在海洋中發現的海洋中有80%到90% , 我們在海洋中發現的海洋是塑膠 , 那麼為什麼我們不把它稱為它是什麼 。
recycling everybody kind of ends their books about being sustainable and greening with the idea of recycling .	回收所有人的書 , 來回收他們的書 , 來回收回收的概念 。
you put something in a bin and you don't have to think about it again .	你把東西放在bin , 你不需要再再思考 。
what is the reality of that ?	到底是什麼 ?
in the united states , less than seven percent of our plastics are recycled .	在美國 , 我們的塑膠收回收不到百分之七 。
and if you really look into it , particularly when it comes to plastic bottles , most of it is only downcycled , or incinerated , or shipped to china .	如果你真的去看它 , 特別是在塑膠瓶裡 , 大部分的只是下降 , 或受到緊密 , 或被運送到中國 。
it is downcycled and turned into lesser things , while a glass bottle can be a glass bottle again or can be used again a plastic bottle can never be a plastic bottle again .	它被下降 , 轉化成較少的東西 , 而玻璃瓶可以再次使用玻璃瓶 , 或可以再次使用塑膠瓶 , 永遠不會是塑膠瓶 。
so this is a big issue for us .	這對我們來說是個大問題 。
another thing that we're looking at and asking people to think about is we've added a fourth r onto the front of the " reduce , reuse , recycle , " three r's , and that is refuse .	另外一件事 , 我們要問人們思考的是 , 我們加入了四個字母的前方 , 回收 , 回收 , 三個r , 那就是拒絕了 。
whenever possible , refuse singleuse and disposable plastics .	無論如何 , 拒絕單一的塑膠 。
alternatives exist ; some of them are very oldschool .	替代方案存在 , 有些是很古老的 。
i myself am now collecting these cool pyrex containers and using those instead of glad and tupperware containers to store food in .	我現在正在收集這些冷酷的preyx容器 , 使用這些 , 而不是玻璃和豐富的收藏者 , 來儲存食物 。
and i know that i am doing a service to myself and my family .	我知道我對自己和家人做服務 。
it's very easy to pick up a stainlesssteel bottle or a glass bottle , if you're traveling and you've forgotten to bring your stainlesssteel bottle and fill that up with water or filtered water , versus purchasing plastic bottled water .	很容易拿起無線電瓶或玻璃瓶 , 如果你在旅行時 , 你就忘了 , 把石油瓶帶進去 , 用水或過濾的水裡 , 用塑膠瓶來填滿塑膠瓶 。
i guess what i want to say to everybody here and i know that you guys know a lot about this issue is that this is a huge problem in the oceans , but this is a problem that we've created as consumers and we can solve .	我猜我想要對大家說些什麼 , 我知道你們對這個議題有很大的問題 , 在海洋中 , 這是我們創造出的消費者 , 我們可以解決的問題 。
we can solve this by raising awareness of the issue and teaching people to choose alternatives .	我們可以藉由提高議題和教導人們選擇替代方案來解決這個問題 。
so whenever possible , to choose alternatives to singleuse plastics .	所以 , 無論如何 , 選擇選擇單一塑膠 。
we can cut the stem tide the stem of this into our oceans and in doing so , save our oceans , save our planet , save ourselves .	我們可以把幹部切割成我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的地球 , 拯救我們自己 。
this demo from pattie maes' lab at mit , spearheaded by pranav mistry was the buzz of ted . it's a wearable device with a projector that paves the way for profound interaction with our environment . imagine " minority report " and then some .	這位來自麻省理工學院的maemaes實驗室 , 由pranre的錯誤推廣 , 是ted的廣場 。 這是一個可行的裝置 , 用一個專案來支付我們環境的深層互動 。 想像一下: 「 少數的報告 」 和一些 。
demo , design , interface design , technology	民主、設計、介面設計、科技設計、科技設計、科技 。
pattie maes and pranav mistry demo sixthsense	親愛的雄性和豬的誤解 , 六度的密度 。
i've been intrigued by this question of whether we could evolve or develop a sixth sense a sense that would give us seamless access and easy access to metainformation or information that may exist somewhere that may be relevant to help us make the right decision about whatever it is that we're coming across .	我對這個問題很感興趣 , 我們是否能演化或發展出六個感知 , 讓我們無力取得、容易取得資訊 , 或在某些地方 , 可能存在的資訊 , 可以幫助我們做出正確的決策 , 不論我們要做什麼 。
and some of you may argue , well , don't today's cell phones do that already ?	在座有些人可能會說 , 今天的手機已經沒用了嗎 ?
but i would say no .	但我會說不 。
when you meet someone here at ted and this is the top networking place , of course , of the year you don't shake somebody's hand and then say , " can you hold on for a moment while i take out my phone and google you ? "	當你在ted見面時 , 這位是上層網絡的地方 , 當然 , 你不喜歡某人的手 , 然後說: 「 你能不能在我拿出手機 , google你嗎 ? 」
or when you go to the supermarket and you're standing there in that huge aisle of different types of toilet papers , you don't take out your cell phone , and open a browser , and go to a website to try to decide which of these different toilet papers is the most ecologically responsible purchase to make .	或者 , 當你去超市時 , 你站在那裡 , 站在那裡 , 不同的廁所論文 , 你不會拿出你的手機 , 打開瀏覽器 , 去一個網站 , 試著決定這些不同的廁所 , 是最負責的任務 。
so we don't really have easy access to all this relevant information that can just help us make optimal decisions about what to do next and what actions to take .	所以我們沒有很容易取得這些相關的資訊 , 只能幫助我們做出最佳的決定 , 來做下一個行動 。
and so my research group at the media lab has been developing a series of inventions to give us access to this information in a sort of easy way , without requiring that the user changes any of their behavior .	所以我在媒體實驗室的研究團體已經開發了一系列的發明 , 以簡單的方式來取得這些資訊 , 不用放棄使用者改變他們的行為 。
and i'm here to unveil our latest effort , and most successful effort so far , which is still very much a work in process .	我在這裡要揭露我們最新的努力 , 最成功的努力 , 目前還在處理過程中 , 也是非常重要的 。
i'm actually wearing the device right now and we've sort of cobbled it together with components that are off the shelf and that , by the way , only cost 350 dollars at this point in time .	我現在正穿著這個裝置 , 然後我們將它結合在一起 , 把它們結合在一起 , 順便說一下 , 當時只有350美元 。
i'm wearing a camera , just a simple webcam , a portable , batterypowered projection system with a little mirror .	我穿著攝影機 , 只是一個簡單的網誌 , 可攜帶、電池的專案系統 , 和一個小鏡子 。
these components communicate to my cell phone in my pocket which acts as the communication and computation device .	這些元件跟我的口袋裡的手機溝通 , 它是溝通和計算設備 。
and in the video here we see my student pranav mistry , who's really the genius who's been implementing and designing this whole system .	在這段影片中 , 我們看到我的學生派對 , 他們真的是執行和設計整個系統的天才 。
and we see how this system lets him walk up to any surface and start using his hands to interact with the information that is projected in front of him .	我們看到這個系統如何讓他走上任何表面 , 開始用他的手來和他面前的資訊互動 。
the system tracks the four significant fingers .	系統追蹤四個指尖 。
in this case , he's wearing simple marker caps that you may recognize .	在這個例子中 , 他穿著簡單的標記帽子 , 你可能知道 。
but if you want a more stylish version you could also paint your nails in different colors .	但如果你想要更輕鬆的版本 , 你也可以在不同的顏色上畫你的細節 。
and the camera basically tracks these four fingers and recognizes any gestures that he's making so he can just go to , for example , a map of long beach , zoom in and out , etc .	相機基本上追蹤了這四個手指 , 辨識出他所製造的任何姿勢 , 例如 , 一個長灘的地圖 , 放大 , 等等 。
the system also recognizes iconic gestures such as the " take a picture " gesture , and then takes a picture of whatever is in front of you .	系統也能辨識出像 「 拍照 」 的圖像 , 然後拍一張你面前的照片 。
and when he then walks back to the media lab , he can just go up to any wall and project all the pictures that he's taken , sort through them and organize them , and resize them , etc . , again using all natural gestures .	當他走回媒體實驗室時 , 他就可以去任何牆壁 , 專案他所拍攝的所有照片 , 包括它們 , 組織起來 , 等等 , 再利用所有自然的姿勢 。
so , some of you most likely were here two years ago and saw the demo by jeff han or some of you may think , " well , doesn't this look like the microsoft surface table ? "	所以 , 有些人可能在兩年前就在這裡 , 看到jfffhan或有些人可能會想: 「 嗯 , 這看起來不像微軟的表面表面桌子嗎 ? 」
and yes , you also interact using natural gestures , both hands , etc .	是的 , 你也用天然的姿勢互動 , 雙手等等 。
but the difference here is that you can use any surface , you can walk to up to any surface , including your hand if nothing else is available and interact with this projected data .	但差別是 , 你可以用任何表面 , 你可以走到任何表面 , 包括你的手 , 如果沒有任何東西可以使用 , 和這個專案資料互動 。
the device is completely portable , and can be . . .	設備完全可攜帶 , 可以 。
so one important difference is that it's totally mobile .	重要的是 , 它是完全移動的 。
another even more important difference is that in mass production this would not cost more tomorrow than today's cell phones and would actually not sort of be a bigger packaging could look a lot more stylish than this version that i'm wearing around my neck .	另一個更重要的差異是 , 在大規模生產中 , 這不會比現今的手機還要多 , 實際上 , 不是更大的包裝 , 可能比我穿著脖子的版本還要多 。
but other than letting some of you live out your fantasy of looking as cool as tom cruise in " minority report , " the reason why we're really excited about this device is that it really can act as one of these sixthsense devices that gives you relevant information about whatever is in front of you .	但除了讓某些人活出你的幻想 , 在《少數報告》中 , 我們對於這個裝置感到興奮的原因是 , 它真的可以扮演這六個感測裝置 , 給你相關的資訊 。
so we see pranav here going into the supermarket and he's shopping for some paper towels .	所以 , 我們在這裡看到豬走進超市 , 他在購買一些紙巾 。
and , as he picks up a product the system can recognize the product that he's picking up , using either image recognition or marker technology , and give him the green light or an orange light .	當他拿起一個產品 , 系統能辨識他拿起的產品時 , 使用圖像辨識或標記技術 , 給他綠光或橘色光 。
he can ask for additional information .	他可以要求更多的資訊 。
so this particular choice here is a particularly good choice , given his personal criteria .	所以這個特定的選擇是特別好的選擇 , 因為他的個人犯罪 。
some of you may want the toilet paper with the most bleach in it rather than the most ecologicallyresponsible choice .	有些人可能想要廁所的紙 , 而不是最有責任的生態選擇 。
if he picks up a book in the bookstore , he can get an amazon rating it gets projected right on the cover of the book .	如果他在書中挑一本書 , 他就能得到亞馬遜的比例 , 把書包放在封面上 。
this is juan's book , our previous speaker , which gets a great rating , by the way , at amazon .	這是jan的書 , 我們先前的演講者 , 順便說一下 , 亞馬遜的比賽 。
and so , pranav turns the page of the book and can then see additional information about the book reader comments , maybe sort of information by his favorite critic , etc .	所以 , 帕爾•羅斯把書頁的頁面 , 可以看到書讀者的內容 , 也許是他最喜歡的批評 , 等等 。
if he turns to a particular page he finds an annotation by maybe an expert of a friend of ours that gives him a little bit of additional information about whatever is on that particular page .	如果他轉到某個特定的頁面 , 他會找到一個信息 , 或許是一位朋友的專家 , 給他一點額外的資訊 , 給他一些特別的頁面 。
reading the newspaper it never has to be outdated .	閱讀報紙 , 不需要被外出 。
you can get video annotations of the event that you're reading about you can get the latest sports scores etc .	你可以得到你所讀到的事件的影片 , 你可以得到最新的運動比例等等 。
this is a more controversial one .	這是更有爭議性的 。
as you interact with someone at ted , maybe you can see a word cloud of the tags , the words that are associated with that person in their blog and personal web pages .	當你和ted的某人互動時 , 也許你能看到一個標籤的字源 , 那些與他們的部落格和個人網頁有關的字母 。
in this case , the student is interested in cameras , etc .	在這個例子中 , 學生對攝影機有興趣 。
on your way to the airport , if you pick up your boarding pass , it can tell you that your flight is delayed , that the gate has changed , etc .	到機場的路上 , 如果你拿起你的板子 , 它可以告訴你你的飛行已經被斷裂了 , 蓋茲已經改變了 。
and , if you need to know what the current time is it's as simple as drawing a watch on your arm .	如果你需要知道現在的時光是什麼樣子 , 就好像在你的手臂上畫看 。
so that's where we're at so far in developing this sixth sense that would give us seamless access to all this relevant information about the things that we may come across .	所以 , 目前我們在開發這個第六個感覺 , 讓我們無法取得這些相關的資訊 , 關於我們可能遇到的事物 。
my student pranav , who's really , like i said , the genius behind this .	我的學生皮爾 , 就像我說的 , 這背後的天才 。
he does deserve a lot of applause because i don't think he's slept much in the last three months , actually .	他的確值得許多讚賞 , 因為我不認為他在過去三個月內睡得太多 。
and his girlfriend is probably not very happy about him either .	他的女友可能也不高興他 。
but it's not perfect yet , it's very much a work in progress .	但這還不完美 , 在進步過程中 , 非常有用 。
and who knows , maybe in another 10 years we'll be here with the ultimate sixth sense brain implant .	誰知道 , 也許在接下來的十年裡 , 我們將來會有第六感官的大腦植入 。
phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	2001年9月11日 , 艾瑞克•羅斯和阿拉伯爾有強大的友誼 。 羅德茲的兒子被殺害了世界貿易中心攻擊在9月11日 , 2001年 , elwafi的兒子zarsauui在那些攻擊中被宣傳 , 並在那些攻擊中提供一個角色 。 希望找到和平 。
culture , global issues , politics	文化、全球性議題、政治、政治 。
9/11 healing: the mothers who found forgiveness , friendship	9/11的治癒:被發現寬恕、友誼的母親 。
phyllis rodriguez: we are here today because of the fact that we have what most people consider an unusual friendship .	菲利斯•羅德里茲:我們今天在這裡 , 是因為我們有大多數人認為一個不尋常的友誼 。
and yet , it feels natural to us now .	然而 , 我們現在感覺很自然 。
i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我首先發現 , 我的兒子在2001年9月11日在世貿中心 。
we didn't know if he had perished yet until 36 hours later .	我們不知道他有沒有被懲罰直到36小時後 。
at the time , we knew that it was political .	當時 , 我們知道這是政治 。
we were afraid of what our country was going to do in the name of our son my husband , orlando , and i and our family .	我們害怕我們的國家會做些什麼 , 在我們的兒子的名字中 , 我和我們的家人 。
and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到它時 , 經過震驚 , 恐怖的震驚 , 我們的生活中最糟糕的爆炸 , 其實 , 我們並沒有被拘留 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾週後 , zacarariamosaui被指出 , 對於恐怖主義有六個數目的疑問 , 美國政府稱他為死刑 , 假如我和我的丈夫和我在對此說話 , 公開討論 。
through that and through human rights groups , we were brought together with several other victims' families .	透過這個和人權團體 , 我們和其他許多受害者的家庭一起聚在一起 。
when i saw aicha in the media , coming over when her son was indicted , and i thought , " what a brave woman .	當我在媒體上看到阿拉伯 , 她兒子被注意的時候 , 我心想: 「 勇敢的女人是什麼 。
someday i want to meet that woman when i'm stronger . "	有一天 , 我想要和那位女士見面 。 」
i was still in deep grief ; i knew i didn't have the strength .	我還在深蒂蒂夫 ; 我知道我沒有力量 。
i knew i would find her someday , or we would find each other .	我知道我有一天會找到她 , 或者我們會互相找到 。
because , when people heard that my son was a victim , i got immediate sympathy .	因為 , 當人們聽到我的兒子是受害者 , 我馬上就有同情 。
but when people learned what her son was accused of , she didn't get that sympathy .	但當人們了解她的兒子被指控時 , 她沒有同情心 。
but her suffering is equal to mine .	但她的苦難和我一樣 。
so we met in november 2002 , and aicha will now tell you how that came about .	我們在2002年11月見面 , 阿卡哈現在會告訴你這怎麼來 。
aicha elwafi: good afternoon , ladies and gentlemen .	aichaelwafi:好的下午 , 各位先生女士 。
i am the mother of zacarias moussaoui .	我是zacariamosaui的母親 。
and i asked the organization of human rights to put me in touch with the parents of the victims .	我問了人類權利的組織 , 讓我和受害者的父母接觸 。
so they introduced me to five families .	所以他們把我介紹給五個家庭 。
and i saw phyllis , and i watched her .	我看到了phyllis , 我看著她 。
she was the only mother in the group .	她是團體中唯一的母親 。
the others were brothers , sisters .	其他人是兄弟姐妹 。
and i saw in her eyes that she was a mother , just like me .	我在她的眼中看到她是個母親 , 就像我一樣 。
i suffered a lot as a mother .	身為一個母親 , 我受苦很多 。
i was married when i was 14 .	我十四歲時結婚 。
i lost a child when i was 15 , a second child when i was 16 .	當我十五歲時 , 我失去了一個孩子 , 第二個小孩 。
so the story with zacarias was too much really .	zacaria的故事太多了 。
and i still suffer , because my son is like he's buried alive .	我仍然受苦 , 因為我的兒子就像是活著的 。
i know she really cried for her son .	我知道她真的哭了她兒子 。
but she knows where he is .	但她知道他在哪裡 。
my son , i don't know where he is .	我兒子不知道他在哪裡 。
i don't know if he's alive . i don't know if he's tortured .	我不知道他是否活著 , 我不知道他是否被害怕 。
i don't know what happened to him .	我不知道他發生了什麼事 。
so that's why i decided to tell my story , so that my suffering is something positive for other women .	這就是為什麼我決定說我的故事 , 所以我的苦難對其他女性來說是正面的 。
for all the women , all the mothers that give life , you can give back , you can change .	對所有女性 , 所有給予生命的母親 , 你可以回饋 , 你可以改變 。
it's up to us women , because we are women , because we love our children .	對我們女性來說 , 因為我們是女性 , 因為我們愛我們的孩子 。
we must be handinhand and do something together .	我們必須是手手 , 一起做些事情 。
it's not against women , it's for us , for us women , for our children .	這不是對女性來說 , 對我們來說 , 對女性來說 , 對我們的孩子來說 。
i talk against violence , against terrorism .	我對抗暴力 , 反對恐怖主義 。
i go to schools to talk to young , muslim girls so they don't accept to be married against their will very young .	我去上學去和年輕的穆斯林女孩談話 , 所以他們不接受結婚 , 來對抗他們的意志很年輕 。
so if i can save one of the young girls , and avoid that they get married and suffer as much as i did , well this is something good .	所以 , 如果我能拯救其中一個年輕女孩 , 避免他們結婚和苦難 , 這就好了 。
this is why i'm here in front of you .	這就是為什麼我在你們面前 。
pr: i would like to say that i have learned so much from aicha , starting with that day we had our very first meeting with other family members which was a very private meeting with security , because it was november 2002 , and , frankly , we were afraid of the superpatriotism of that time in the country those of us family members .	pr:我想說 , 我從阿拉哈學過這麼多 , 從那天開始 , 我們和其他家庭成員一起參加了一場非常私人的會議 , 因為那是2002年11月 , 坦白說 , 我們害怕那個時代的超級抗議主義主義 。
but we were all so nervous .	但我們都很緊張 。
" why does she want to meet us ? "	「 為什麼她想要見我們 ? 」
and then she was nervous .	然後她很緊張 。
" why did we want to meet her ? "	「 我們為什麼要見她 ? 」
what did we want from each other ?	我們對彼此想要什麼 ?
before we knew each others' names , or anything , we had embraced and wept .	在我們認識彼此的名字之前 , 或任何東西之前 , 我們都擁抱了 。
then we sat in a circle with support , with help , from people experienced in this kind of reconciliation .	接著 , 我們和支持團結在一起 , 透過幫助 , 從人們體驗到這種關聯性 。
and aicha started , and she said , " i don't know if my son is guilty or innocent , but i want to tell you how sorry i am for what happened to your families .	阿卡哈開始 , 她說: 「 我不知道我的兒子是罪惡或無辜 , 但我想告訴你們 , 我對你的家庭有多抱歉 。
i know what it is to suffer , and i feel that if there is a crime , a person should be tried fairly and punished . "	我知道 , 受苦是什麼 , 我覺得如果有犯罪 , 一個人應該很公平地嘗試和懲罰 。 」
but she reached out to us in that way , and it was , i'd like to say , it was an icebreaker .	但她在那方面向我們伸出去 , 我想說 , 這是個冰箱 。
and what happened then is we all told our stories , and we all connected as human beings .	接下來發生的事是 , 我們都告訴我們的故事 , 我們都與人類連結在一起 。
by the end of the afternoon it was about three hours after lunch we'd felt as if we'd known each other forever .	到午餐後 , 大約是午餐後的三小時 , 我們就覺得我們永遠都知道 。
now what i learned from her , is a woman , not only who could be so generous under these present circumstances and what it was then , and what was being done to her son , but the life she's had .	我從她身上學到的 , 是女性 , 不僅在現場環境下有這麼慷慨的情況下 , 以及當時的狀況 , 以及她兒子所做的事 , 還有她所擁有的生命 。
i never had met someone with such a hard life , from such a totally different culture and environment from my own .	我從來沒有遇過這種艱難生活的人 , 來自我自己的文化和環境 。
and i feel that we have a special connection , which i value very much .	我覺得我們有特殊的連結 , 我非常重視 。
and i think it's all about being afraid of the other , but making that step and then realizing , " hey , this wasn't so hard .	我認為這一切都是害怕別人的 , 但讓這步驟 , 然後意識到: 「 嘿 , 這不太困難 。
who else can i meet that i don't know , or that i'm so different from ? "	誰可以見到我不知道的 , 或我是如此不同 ? 」
so , aicha , do you have a couple of words for conclusion ?	所以 , 阿卡哈 , 你有幾個字符合結論嗎 ?
because our time is up .	因為我們的時間很高 。
aw: i wanted to say that we have to try to know other people , the other .	aw:我想說 , 我們必須試著認識別人 , 另一個人 。
you have to be generous , and your hearts must be generous , your mind must be generous .	你必須是慷慨的 , 你的心必須是慷慨的 , 你的心智一定是慷慨的 。
you must be tolerant .	你一定要被移除 。
you have to fight against violence .	你必須對抗暴力 。
and i hope that someday we'll all live together in peace and respecting each other .	我希望有一天我們都一起生活在和平和尊重彼此 。

and i'm sure you'll feel that it's from a safe source .	我相信你會覺得它來自安全來源 。

what if it was from a source like this ?	如果它來自像這樣的來源呢 ?
then statistics would actually say that half of you would now be suffering with diarrhea .	統計數據會說 , 現在有一半的人會受腹瀉受苦 。

by the way , since i've been speaking , another 13 , 000 people around the world are suffering now with diarrhea .	順便說一提 , 自從我說話 , 世界上有13 , 000人現在受到腹瀉受苦 。

i invented lifesaver bottle because i got angry .	我發明了生命的瓶子 , 因為我生氣了 。
i , like most of you , was sitting down , the day after christmas in 2004 , when i was watching the devastating news of the asian tsunami as it rolled in , playing out on tv .	我和大部分人一樣 , 坐在2004年聖誕節後一天 , 當我看著亞洲海嘯的破壞新聞時 , 我在電視上扮演電視 。
the days and weeks that followed , people fleeing to the hills , being forced to drink contaminated water or face death .	接下來的日子和幾個星期 , 人們逃到山丘 , 被迫喝污染的水或死 。
that really stuck with me .	我真的很困惑 。

do you know it took five days to get water to the superdome ?	你知道嗎 ? 花了五天才能把水帶到超級室裡嗎 ?
people were shooting each other on the streets for tv sets and water .	人們在街上射擊彼此 , 為了電視和水 。

now i spent a lot of time in my garage , over the next weeks and months , and also in my kitchen much to the dismay of my wife .	現在我花了很多時間在我的車庫裡 , 在接下來的幾個星期和幾個月內 , 我廚房的廚房和妻子的差異 。

okay , now for the science bit .	好吧 , 現在 , 科學的一部分 。
before lifesaver , the best hand filters were only capable of filtering down to about 200 nanometers .	在生命saver之前 , 最好的濾器只能過濾到200奈米 。
the smallest bacteria is about 200 nanometers .	最小的細菌大約是200奈米 。
so a 200nanometer bacteria is going to get through a 200nanometer hole .	所以 , 一個200奈米的細菌將會經過200奈米的洞 。
the smallest virus , on the other hand , is about 25 nanometers .	另一方面 , 最小的病毒大約是25奈米 。
so that's definitely going to get through those 200 nanometer holes .	這絕對是要穿過那200奈米洞 。
lifesaver pores are 15 nanometers .	生命總共有15奈米 。
so nothing is getting through .	所以 , 一切都沒有 。

the lifesaver bottle works really simply .	生命的瓶子真的很簡單 。

okay . there we go .	好吧 , 我們去了 。
give it a few pumps . okay ?	給它一些泵 , 好嗎 ?
that's all that's necessary .	這就是必要的 。
now as soon as i pop the teat , sterile drinking water is going to come out .	一旦我把茶吃掉 , 很穩定的飲用水會出去 。

okay . lifesaver bottle is used by thousands of people around the world .	好吧 , 世界各地數以千計的人使用 。

and when it's expired , using failsafe technology , the system will shut off , protecting the user .	當它啟發時 , 使用失敗的技術 , 系統會關閉 , 保護使用者 。

so let's look at the applications .	咱們來看看應用 。
traditionally , in a crisis , what do we do ?	傳統上 , 在危機中 , 我們該怎麼做 ?
then , after a few weeks , we set up camps .	接著 , 幾週後 , 我們開始營地 。
and people are forced to come into the camps to get their safe drinking water .	人們被迫進入營地 , 來取得安全飲用水 。
what happens when 20 , 000 people congregate in a camp ?	當兩萬人聚集在營地時會發生什麼事呢 ?
diseases spread . more resources are required .	疾病散播 , 更多資源都需要 。
the problem just becomes selfperpetuating .	問題就變成了自我分散 。
but by thinking differently , and shipping these , people can stay put .	但 , 用不同的方式思考 , 並運送這些 , 人們可以留下 。
they can make their own sterile drinking water , and start to get on with rebuilding their homes and their lives .	他們可以自己飲用水 , 開始重建他們的家和生活 。
now , it doesn't require a natural disaster for this to work .	現在 , 它不需要一個自然災難來工作 。
using the old thinking , of national infrastructure and pipe work , is too expensive .	利用國家基礎設施和pipe工作的舊思考 , 太昂貴了 。
when you run the numbers on a calculator , you run out of noughts .	當你在計算機上進行計算機時 , 你就跑出笑聲 。
so here is the " thinking different " bit .	這就是 「 思考不一樣 」 。
instead of shipping water , and using manmade processes to do it , let's use mother nature . she's got a fantastic system .	不用運輸水 , 用人造程序來做 , 咱們用大自然 。 她有很棒的系統 。
she picks the water up from there , desalinates it , for free , transports it over there , and dumps it onto the mountains , rivers , and streams .	她從那裡挑出水 , 把水放到那裡 , 把它放到山上 , 把它丟在山上 , 河流和溪流上 。
and where do people live ? near water .	人們住在哪裡 ? 附近的水 。
all we've go to do is make it sterile . how do we do that ?	我們要做的就是讓它變得很穩定 。 我們該怎麼做 ?
well , we could use the lifesaver bottle .	嗯 , 我們可以使用生命的瓶子 。
or we could use one of these .	或者 , 我們可以使用其中一個 。
the same technology , in a jerry can .	同樣的科技 , 在猶太人可以 。
this will process 25 , 000 liters of water ; that's good enough for a family of four , for three years .	這會處理25000公升的水 , 這足以足夠四、三年來的家庭 。
and how much does it cost ?	它的成本有多少 ?
about half a cent a day to run .	每天只有半分之一的跑步 。
so , by thinking differently , and processing water at the point of use , mothers and children no longer have to walk four hours a day to collect their water .	所以 , 用不同的方式思考 , 在使用時期 , 母親和兒童不再需要每天四小時才能收集他們的水 。
they can get it from a source nearby .	它們可以從附近的來源 。
so with just eight billion dollars , we can hit the millennium goal's target of halving the number of people without access to safe drinking water .	所以 , 只有八十億美金 , 我們可以撞上千禧年的目標 , 讓人們無法取得安全飲用水 。
to put that into context , the u . k . government spends about 12 billion pounds a year on foreign aid .	為了將這點放到情境上 , 美國政府每年花大約12億英鎊的外國援助 。
but why stop there ?	但為什麼停下來 ?
with 20 billion dollars , everyone can have access to safe drinking water .	有20億美元 , 每個人都能取得安全飲用水 。
so the threeandahalf billion people that suffer every year as a result , and the two million kids that die every year , will live .	所以每年的三十五億人每年受苦 , 每年有兩百萬個孩子死亡 , 將會活下來 。
paddy ashdown claims that we are living in a moment in history where power is changing in ways it never has before . in a spellbinding talk at tedxbrussels he outlines the three major global shifts that he sees coming .	在歷史上 , 廣泛宣稱我們生活在歷史上 , 權力正在改變 。 在tedxussel的演講中 , 他將他所看到的三項重大的全球轉變 。
foreign policy , global issues , politics , world cultures	外國政策、全球議題、政治、世界文化文化、世界文化 。
paddy ashdown: the global power shift	adaddyashown:全球的權力轉變 。
there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在19世紀末 , 有一首詩被一首非常著名的英語詩人寫作 。
it was said to echo in churchill's brain in the 1930s .	在1930年代 , 伊斯蘭的大腦被告知 。
and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die . "	首詩說: 「 夏天 , 夏天 , 和蒸汽的流動 , 我聽到一個遙遠的鼓吹 , 像一個夢中、附近、附近的聲音 , 在地球的路上 , 親愛的朋友和食物 , 很快地到來 , 士兵飛行 。 」
those who are interested in poetry , the poem is " a shropshire lad " written by a . e . housman .	那些對詩有興趣的人 , 詩是 「 一名商店女士 」 寫的 。 奧斯曼 。
but what housman understood , and you hear it in the symphonies of nielsen too , was that the long , hot , silvan summers of stability of the 19th century were coming to a close , and that we were about to move into one of those terrifying periods of history when power changes .	但 , 荷蘭人也知道 , 在尼爾森的物理過程中 , 是19世紀的穩定階段 , 史蒂芬•夏天 , 我們將要搬到其中一個恐怖的時代 。
and these are always periods , ladies and gentlemen , accompanied by turbulence , and all too often by blood .	這些都是經常的時期 , 女士們先生們 , 被暴風暴所伴隨著 , 通常都是血液 。
and my message for you is that i believe we are condemned , if you like , to live at just one of those moments in history when the gimbals upon which the established order of power is beginning to change and the new look of the world , the new powers that exist in the world , are beginning to take form .	我對你們的訊息是 , 我相信我們是被認定的 , 如果你想要活在歷史上 , 只有一個時刻 , 當gimbal發出的力量開始改變和世界的新角度 , 現有的新力量就開始採取形式 。
and these are and we see it very clearly today nearly always highly turbulent times , highly difficult times , and all too often very bloody times .	今天我們很明顯地看到 , 幾乎永遠都很緊張 , 很困難的時期 , 很多時候都很血 。
by the way , it happens about once every century .	順便一提 , 每一世紀就發生了 。
you might argue that the last time it happened and that's what housman felt coming and what churchill felt too was that when power passed from the old nations , the old powers of europe , across the atlantic to the new emerging power of the united states of america the beginning of the american century .	你可能會說 , 上次發生了 , 那是霍華曼的感受 , 教會也感覺到 , 當權力從古老的國家 , 歐洲的舊權力 , 橫跨大西洋 , 到美國的新興力量 , 美國開始 。
and of course , into the vacuum where the tooold european powers used to be were played the two bloody catastrophes of the last century the one in the first part and the one in the second part: the two great world wars .	當然 , 在真空中 , 當時的歐洲權力曾經扮演了上個世紀的二個血液災難 , 第二個部分:兩個偉大的世界大戰爭 。
mao zedong used to refer to them as the european civil wars , and it's probably a more accurate way of describing them .	馬里•0多曾經把他們視為歐洲內戰 , 可能是更準確的描述他們 。
well , ladies and gentlemen , we live at one of those times .	各位先生女士 , 我們住在其中一次 。
but for us , i want to talk about three factors today .	但對我們來說 , 我今天要談談三個因素 。
and the first of these , the first two of these , is about a shift in power .	首先 , 首先 , 這兩種是權力的轉變 。
and the second is about some new dimension which i want to refer to , which has never quite happened in the way it's happening now .	第二個是關於一些新的維度 , 我想要重新思考 , 這從來沒有發生在它正在發生的方式 。
but let's talk about the shifts of power that are occurring to the world .	但讓我們來談談世界上的力量轉變 。
and what is happening today is , in one sense , frightening because it's never happened before .	今天發生的事是 , 一方面來說 , 令人害怕 , 因為它從來沒有發生過 。
we have seen lateral shifts of power the power of greece passed to rome and the power shifts that occurred during the european civilizations but we are seeing something slightly different .	我們看過之後的力量轉變了希臘的力量 , 在歐洲文明中發生的權力轉變 , 但我們看到一些不一樣的東西 。
for power is not just moving laterally from nation to nation .	權力不僅僅是從國家到國家 。
it's also moving vertically .	它也在垂直移動 。
what's happening today is that the power that was encased , held to accountability , held to the rule of law , within the institution of the nation state has now migrated in very large measure onto the global stage .	今天的情況是 , 被迫被監禁的權力 , 抵制法律的制度 , 在國家制度的制度中 , 已經遷移到全球階段非常大的衡量 。
the globalization of power we talk about the globalization of markets , but actually it's the globalization of real power .	全球化的權力 , 我們談論市場的全球化 , 但實際上是真正的力量 。
and where , at the nation state level that power is held to accountability subject to the rule of law , on the international stage it is not .	在國家國家的層面上 , 權力是對法律規則的負責主題 , 在國際舞台上 , 不是 。
the international stage and the global stage where power now resides: the power of the internet , the power of the satellite broadcasters , the power of the money changers this vast moneygoround that circulates now 32 times the amount of money necessary for the trade it's supposed to be there to finance the money changers , if you like , the financial speculators that have brought us all to our knees quite recently , the power of the multinational corporations now developing budgets often bigger than mediumsized countries .	國際階段和全球階段 , 現在的權力是:網路的力量 , 衛星廣播者的力量 , 金錢改變者的力量 , 這種大量的金錢在交易中 , 要花費了32倍的金錢 , 它應該要在交易上取得金錢改變 , 如果你喜歡 , 金融的推動者 , 如同你所謂的財務推動者 , 最近我們所有人都帶給我們的膝蓋爾茲 。
these live in a global space which is largely unregulated , not subject to the rule of law , and in which people may act free of constraint .	這些生活在一個大規模的全球空間中 , 沒有規範法律的規則 , 人們可能不會選擇限制 。
now that suits the powerful up to a moment .	現在 , 這個裝置是一瞬間的 。
it's always suitable for those who have the most power to operate in spaces without constraint , but the lesson of history is that , sooner or later , unregulated space space not subject to the rule of law becomes populated , not just by the things you wanted international trade , the internet , etc . but also by the things you don't want international criminality , international terrorism .	對那些沒有限制的空間中最有權力的人來說 , 但歷史的課題是 , 不久後 , 沒有規定的空間 , 不只只是你想要國際貿易、網際網路 , 等等 , 除了你不喜歡國際犯罪、國際犯罪、國際恐怖主義的東西 。
the revelation of 9/11 is that even if you are the most powerful nation on earth , nevertheless , those who inhabit that space can attack you even in your most iconic of cities one bright september morning .	911事件的揭示 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 不管哪些地方都能攻擊你 , 甚至在你最明亮的城市早上攻擊你 。
it's said that something like 60 percent of the four million dollars that was taken to fund 9/11 actually passed through the institutions of the twin towers which 9/11 destroyed .	它說 , 大約有60%的400萬美金 , 由於911的資金基金 , 實際上通過兩座塔的機構 , 9/11摧毀了 。
you see , our enemies also use this space the space of mass travel , the internet , satellite broadcasters to be able to get around their poison , which is about destroying our systems and our ways .	我們的敵人也使用這個空間 , 大眾旅行、網路、衛星廣播者 , 來到他們的毒品 , 來解決我們的系統和路徑 。
sooner or later , sooner or later , the rule of history is that where power goes governance must follow .	很快地 , 或後來 , 歷史的規則是 , 權力在哪裡要遵循 。
and if it is therefore the case , as i believe it is , that one of the phenomenon of our time is the globalization of power , then it follows that one of the challenges of our time is to bring governance to the global space .	如果它存在於這個情況 , 如同我相信 , 我們時代的一個現象之一就是全球化 , 那麼 , 我們的時間的挑戰是將國際空間帶進來 。
and i believe that the decades ahead of us now will be to a greater or lesser extent turbulent the more or less we are able to achieve that aim: to bring governance to the global space .	我相信 , 數十年來 , 我們現在會變得更大或更少 , 我們能達成目標:將國際空間帶進國際空間 。
now notice , i'm not talking about government .	注意到 , 我不是在談政府 。
i'm not talking about setting up some global democratic institution .	我不是在談全球民主機構 。
my own view , by the way , ladies and gentlemen , is that this is unlikely to be done by spawning more u . n . institutions .	順便說一提 , 各位先生女士們 , 這不太可能是用更多的聯合國機構來做 。
if we didn't have the u . n . , we'd have to invent it .	如果我們沒有聯合國 , 我們必須發明它 。
the world needs an international forum .	世界需要國際論壇 。
it needs a means by which you can legitimize international action .	它需要一個意義 , 可以合法化國際行動 。
but when it comes to governance of the global space , my guess is this won't happen through the creation of more u . n . institutions .	但當它來到全球空間的治理時 , 我的猜測是 , 這不會發生在美國憲法的創造中 。
it will actually happen by the powerful coming together and making treatybased systems , treatybased agreements , to govern that global space .	實際上 , 強大的成果會發生 , 以治療基礎的系統、治療協議 , 來管理這個全球空間 。
and if you look , you can see them happening , already beginning to emerge .	如果你看 , 你可以看到它們正在發生 , 已經開始出現 。
the world trade organization: treatybased organization , entirely treatybased , and yet , powerful enough to hold even the most powerful , the united states , to account if necessary .	世界貿易組織:治療基礎組織 , 完全依賴 , 然而 , 強大的權力 , 甚至能維持最強大、美國 , 如果必要的話 。
kyoto: the beginnings of struggling to create a treatybased organization .	kyoto:努力創造一個治療組織的開端 。
the g20: we know now that we have to put together an institution which is capable of bringing governance to that financial space for financial speculation .	g20:我們現在知道 , 我們必須組合一套機構 , 可以將金融空間帶給金融空間 。
and that's what the g20 is , a treatybased institution .	這就是g20的樣子 , 以治療為基礎的機構
now there's a problem there , and we'll come back to it in a minute , which is that if you bring the most powerful together to make the rules in treatybased institutions , to fill that governance space , then what happens to the weak who are left out ?	這裡有個問題 , 一分鐘後 , 我們會回來 , 那就是 , 如果你把最強大的結合在一起 , 把規則放在治療的制度上 , 來填補那些治理空間 , 那麼最弱的人會發生什麼事 ?
and that's a big problem , and we'll return to it in just a second .	這是個大問題 , 我們會一秒鐘回來 。
so there's my first message , that if you are to pass through these turbulent times more or less turbulently , then our success in doing that will in large measure depend on our capacity to bring sensible governance to the global space .	所以 , 我的第一個訊息是 , 如果你要通過這些時間或較少 , 我們的成功會在大規模的測量能力上取決於我們對全球空間的敏銳治理 。
and watch that beginning to happen .	看看那開始發生 。
my second point is , and i know i don't have to talk to an audience like this about such a thing , but power is not just shifting vertically , it's also shifting horizontally .	我的第二點是 , 我知道我不需要和像這樣的觀眾談話 , 但權力不僅僅是轉換 , 它也正在轉變 。
you might argue that the story , the history of civilizations , has been civilizations gathered around seas with the first ones around the mediterranean , the more recent ones in the ascendents of western power around the atlantic .	你可能會說 , 文明的歷史 , 文明的歷史一直被文明聚集在海平面上 , 在地中海中 , 最近期的西方權力在大西洋中 。
well it seems to me that we're now seeing a fundamental shift of power , broadly speaking , away from nations gathered around the atlantic [seaboard] to the nations gathered around the pacific rim .	對我來說 , 我們現在看到了一場權力的轉變 , 廣泛地說話 , 從大西洋棋的國家聚集到太平洋河的各地 。
now that begins with economic power , but that's the way it always begins .	這從經濟力量開始 , 但它總是開始 。
you already begin to see the development of foreign policies , the augmentation of military budgets occurring in the other growing powers in the world .	你已經開始看到外交政策的發展 , 軍事預算的增長 , 在世界上其他成長的力量 。
i think actually this is not so much a shift from the west to the east ; something different is happening .	我認為這不是從西方轉變到東部的轉變 ; 不同的事情正在發生 。
my guess is , for what it's worth , is that the united states will remain the most powerful nation on earth for the next 10 years , 15 , but the context in which she holds her power has now radically altered ; it has radically changed .	我的猜測是 , 值得的 , 美國會維持未來十年最強大的國家 , 十五年來 , 但她的權力已經徹底改變 ; 它已經徹底改變了 。
we are coming out of 50 years , most unusual years , of history in which we have had a totally monopolar world , in which every compass needle for or against has to be referenced by its position to washington a world bestrode by a single colossus .	我們從50年來到來 , 大部分年來 , 歷史中 , 我們有著完全相反的世界 , 每一針都要被安慰的位置來接觸到華盛頓世界最好的位置 。
but that's not a usual case in history .	但這不是歷史上常見的例子 。
in fact , what's now emerging is the much more normal case of history .	事實上 , 現在的新興是歷史的正常情況 。
you're beginning to see the emergence of a multipolar world .	你開始看到一個多元世界的出現 。
up until now , the united states has been the dominant feature of our world .	直到現在 , 美國一直是我們世界的主要特徵 。
they will remain the most powerful nation , but they will be the most powerful nation in an increasingly multipolar world .	他們會維持最強大的國家 , 但他們會成為越來越多世界的強大國家 。
and you begin to see the alternative centers of power building up in china , of course , though my own guess is that china's ascent to greatness is not smooth .	當然 , 你開始看到中國的電力建設中心 , 雖然我自己的猜測是中國的集中 , 不是空氣 。
it's going to be quite grumpy as china begins to democratize her society after liberalizing her economy .	隨著中國開始將她的社會民主化 , 在自由化經濟之後 , 會變得很痛苦 。
but that's a subject of a different discussion .	但那是不同的討論主題 。
you see india , you see brazil .	你看到印度 , 你看到巴西 。
you see increasingly that the world now looks actually , for us europeans , much more like europe in the 19th century .	你愈來愈發現 , 世界現在看起來真的是歐洲人 , 更像19世紀的歐洲人 。
europe in the 19th century: a great british foreign secretary , lord canning , used to describe it as the " european concert of powers . "	在19世紀 , 歐洲:一個偉大的英國外交秘書 , 洛杉磯 , 曾經描述它是《歐洲的權力協會》 。
there was a balance , a fivesided balance .	有一個平衡 , 一個五個平衡 。
britain always played to the balance .	英國總是扮演平衡 。
if paris got together with berlin , britain got together with vienna and rome to provide a counterbalance .	如果巴黎和柏林合作 , 英國和維納和羅馬一起合作 , 來提供對抗性 。
now notice , in a period which is dominated by a monopolar world , you have fixed alliances nato , the warsaw pact .	注意到 , 在一個獨立的世界中 , 你已經修正了一系列的聯盟 , 安局 。
a fixed polarity of power means fixed alliances .	一個固定的權力 , 意味著固定的聯盟 。
but a multiple polarity of power means shifting and changing alliances .	但有多種的力量 , 意味著轉變和改變盟友 。
and that's the world we're coming into , in which we will increasingly see that our alliances are not fixed .	這就是我們來到的世界 , 我們會越來越發現我們的盟友不是固定的 。
canning , the great british foreign secretary once said , " britain has a common interest , but no common allies . "	蠟燭 , 英國外交秘書曾經說過: 「 英國有共同的利益 , 但沒有共通的盟友 。 」
and we will see increasingly that even we in the west will reach out , have to reach out , beyond the cozy circle of the atlantic powers to make alliances with others if we want to get things done in the world .	我們會越來越看到 , 即使在西方的西方 , 必須達到 , 遠遠超過大西洋力量的共識圈 , 讓其他人和其他人合作 , 如果我們想在世界做事 。
note , that when we went into libya , it was not good enough for the west to do it alone ; we had to bring others in .	記住 , 當我們進入利比亞時 , 西方不夠好 , 不夠好 。 我們必須把其他人帶進來 。
we had to bring , in this case , the arab league in .	在這個例子中 , 我們必須帶領阿拉伯聯盟 。
my guess is iraq and afghanistan are the last times when the west has tried to do it themselves , and we haven't succeeded .	我的猜測是伊拉克和阿富汗 , 當西方嘗試自己時 , 我們就沒成功了 。
my guess is that we're reaching the beginning of the end of 400 years i say 400 years because it's the end of the ottoman empire of the hegemony of western power , western institutions and western values .	我的猜想是 , 我們在400年末的開端 , 我說了400年 , 因為這是西方權力的終點 , 西方機構和西方價值觀 。
you know , up until now , if the west got its act together , it could propose and dispose in every corner of the world .	你知道 , 直到現在 , 如果西方的行動 , 它可以在世界各角落中推出和分離 。
but that's no longer true .	但這不再是真實的 。
take the last financial crisis after the second world war .	以第二次世界大戰後的財務危機為例 。
the west got together the bretton woods institution , world bank , international monetary fund the problem solved .	西方國家團結了布雷頓木材機構 , 世界銀行、國際網路資金 , 解決問題 。
now we have to call in others .	現在我們必須打電話給別人 。
now we have to create the g20 .	現在我們必須創造g20 。
now we have to reach beyond the cozy circle of our western friends .	現在我們必須超越西方朋友的共同圈 。
let me make a prediction for you , which is probably even more startling .	讓我預測一下 , 這可能更令人驚訝 。
i suspect we are now reaching the end of 400 years when western power was enough .	我懷疑我們現在要達到400年的終點當西方權力足夠 。
people say to me , " the chinese , of course , they'll never get themselves involved in peacemaking , multilateral peacemaking around the world . "	人們對我說: 「 中國 , 當然 , 他們永遠不會自己參與和平 , 跨國和世界各地的和平 。 」
oh yes ? why not ?	喔 ? 為什麼不 ?
how many chinese troops are serving under the blue beret , serving under the blue flag , serving under the u . n . command in the world today ?	在藍色旗下 , 有多少中國軍隊都在服務藍色旗幟下 , 在聯合國的指令下服務 ?
how many americans ? 11 .	有多少美國人 ? 11 。
what is the largest naval contingent tackling the issue of somali pirates ?	哪些是最大的罪犯 , 針對索馬利海盜的問題 ?
the chinese naval contingent .	中國航海的內容 。
of course they are , they are a mercantilist nation .	當然 , 他們是商業主義國家 。
they want to keep the sea lanes open .	他們想要讓海浪開放 。
increasingly , we are going to have to do business with people with whom we do not share values , but with whom , for the moment , we share common interests .	越來越多 , 我們必須和我們沒有共享價值的人做生意 , 但同時 , 我們有共同利益 。
it's a whole new different way of looking at the world that is now emerging .	這是一個全新的看法 , 全新的看待世界 。
and here's the third factor , which is totally different .	第三個因素 , 完全不同 。
today in our modern world , because of the internet , because of the kinds of things people have been talking about here , everything is connected to everything .	現今 , 在現代世界 , 因為網路 , 因為人們在談論的事物 , 一切都與所有事物連結在一起 。
we are now interdependent .	我們現在是互相依賴的 。
we are now interlocked , as nations , as individuals , in a way which has never been the case before , never been the case before .	我們現在被關閉 , 身為國家 , 身為個體 , 以以前從來沒有發生過的案例 。
the interrelationship of nations , well it's always existed .	國家的國際關係總是存在 。
diplomacy is about managing the interrelationship of nations .	外交是把國際國際國際的國際交互關注 。
but now we are intimately locked together .	但現在我們終於被鎖在一起 。
you get swine flu in mexico , it's a problem for charles de gaulle airport 24 hours later .	你在墨西哥游泳 , 它在24小時後就有一個問題 。
lehman brothers goes down , the whole lot collapses .	萊曼兄弟會下降 , 整個崩潰 。
there are fires in the steppes of russia , food riots in africa .	在俄羅斯的步驟中 , 糧食暴行 。
we are all now deeply , deeply , deeply interconnected .	我們現在都深深地 , 深深的連結 。
and what that means is the idea of a nation state acting alone , not connected with others , not working with others , is no longer a viable proposition .	意思是 , 一個國家制度的概念 , 不用與其他人聯繫 , 而不是與其他人合作 , 不再是一個可見的建議 。
because the actions of a nation state are neither confined to itself , nor is it sufficient for the nation state itself to control its own territory , because the effects outside the nation state are now beginning to affect what happens inside them .	因為國家國家的行動也沒有限制自己 , 對國家制度來說 , 不足以控制自己的地位 , 因為在國家外的效果開始影響到內在發生的事 。
i was a young soldier in the last of the small empire wars of britain .	我是英國最後一場小型帝國戰爭的士兵 。
at that time , the defense of my country was about one thing and one thing only: how strong was our army , how strong was our air force , how strong was our navy and how strong were our allies .	那時 , 我國家的防禦是一件事 , 只有一件事:我們的軍隊有多強壯 , 我們的空軍 , 我們的航空力量有多強大 , 以及我們的盟友有多強大 。
that was when the enemy was outside the walls .	敵人在牆外 。
now the enemy is inside the walls .	敵人在牆裡 。
now if i want to talk about the defense of my country , i have to speak to the minister of health because pandemic disease is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of agriculture because food security is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of industry because the fragility of our hitech infrastructure is now a point of attack for our enemies as we see from cyber warfare i have to speak to the minister of home affairs because who has entered my country , who lives in that terraced house in that inner city has a direct effect on what happens in my country as we in london saw in the 7/7 bombings .	現在 , 如果我想談談我的國家防禦 , 我必須和健康部長談談 , 因為流行疾病對我安全的威脅 , 我必須跟農業的總理說話 , 因為食物安全對我的安全感 , 我必須和工業部長談談 , 因為我們的希格斯基礎建設的脆弱 , 正是我們在國內的敵人 , 因為在我家中看到的 , 我們在家中看到的戰爭 。
it's no longer the case that the security of a country is simply a matter for its soldiers and its ministry of defense .	它不再是國家安全的情況 , 只是它的士兵和國防部長的重要性 。
it's its capacity to lock together its institutions .	它是它的能力 , 把它的機構鎖在一起 。
and this tells you something very important .	這告訴你們一些很重要的事 。
it tells you that , in fact , our governments , vertically constructed , constructed on the economic model of the industrial revolution vertical hierarchy , specialization of tasks , command structures have got the wrong structures completely .	它告訴各位 , 事實上 , 我們的政府 , 垂直建構了工業革命的經濟模式 , 建構了工業革命的經濟模式 , 特殊的任務 , 指令結構完全有錯誤的結構 。
you in business know that the paradigm structure of our time , ladies and gentlemen , is the network .	你在商業中知道 , 我們時代的範例結構 , 先生女士 , 是網路 。
it's your capacity to network that matters , both within your governments and externally .	這是你對網路的能力 , 在你的政府和外部都很重要 。
so here is ashdown's third law .	這裡是ashown第三法則 。
by the way , don't ask me about ashdown's first law and second law because i haven't invented those yet ; it always sounds better if there's a third law , doesn't it ?	順便說一提 , 不要問我hshdn的第一法律和第二法律 , 因為我還沒發明這些 ; 如果有第三法律 , 聽起來更好嗎 ?
ashdown's third law is that in the modern age , where everything is connected to everything , the most important thing about what you can do is what you can do with others .	阿什諾的第三法則是 , 在現代時代 , 一切都與所有事物連結 , 最重要的是你能做的事是你能和其他人做的事 。
the most important bit about your structure whether you're a government , whether you're an army regiment , whether you're a business is your docking points , your interconnectors , your capacity to network with others .	最重要的是 , 你的結構是否是政府 , 不論你是軍隊監控 , 不管你是企業 , 你的內部人 , 你的網路和其他人的能力 。
you understand that in industry ; governments don't .	你知道在產業中 , 政府不會 。
but now one final thing .	但最後一件事 。
if it is the case , ladies and gentlemen and it is that we are now locked together in a way that has never been quite the same before , then it's also the case that we share a destiny with each other .	如果是這個案例 , 先生女士們 , 我們現在被鎖在一起 , 以以前從來沒有相同的方式 , 那也是我們和彼此共享絕望的案例 。
suddenly and for the very first time , collective defense , the thing that has dominated us as the concept of securing our nations , is no longer enough .	突然間 , 一開始 , 集體防禦 , 把我們當作秘密國家的概念 , 不再夠了 。
it used to be the case that if my tribe was more powerful than their tribe , i was safe ; if my country was more powerful than their country , i was safe ; my alliance , like nato , was more powerful than their alliance , i was safe .	以前 , 如果我的部落比他們的部落更強大 , 我很安全 ; 如果我的國家比他們的國家更加安全 ; 我的盟友 , 比如nato , 比他們的盟友更強大 , 我更安全 。
it is no longer the case .	它不再是這樣 。
the advent of the interconnectedness and of the weapons of mass destruction means that , increasingly , i share a destiny with my enemy .	大規模毀滅的時代和武器的進展 , 意味著 , 越來越多 , 我和敵人分享了一個命運 。
when i was a diplomat negotiating the disarmament treaties with the soviet union in geneva in the 1970s , we succeeded because we understood we shared a destiny with them .	當我是一個外交官協商在1970年代和蘇聯聯聯聯盟時 , 我們成功了 , 因為我們知道我們和他們分享了命運 。
collective security is not enough .	集體安全不夠 。
peace has come to northern ireland because both sides realized that the zerosum game couldn't work .	和平來到北愛爾蘭 , 因為兩邊都意識到 , 零和遊戲無法運作 。
they shared a destiny with their enemies .	他們和敵人共享了命運 。
one of the great barriers to peace in the middle east is that both sides , both israel and , i think , the palestinians , do not understand that they share a collective destiny .	中東的一個偉大障礙之一是以色列和平的兩邊 , 我認為 , 巴勒斯坦人 , 不了解他們有共同的命運 。
and so suddenly , ladies and gentlemen , what has been the proposition of visionaries and poets down the ages becomes something we have to take seriously as a matter of public policy .	所以 , 突然間 , 女士們先生們 , 正是視覺和詩人的建議 , 成為我們必須認真的公共政策 。
i started with a poem , i'll end with one .	我從一首詩開始 , 最後會結束 。
the great poem of john donne's .	約翰•唐納的偉大詩 。
" send not for whom the bell tolls . "	「 不要為誰捐錢 。 」
the poem is called " no man is an island . "	詩叫做 「 沒有人是島嶼 」 。
and it goes: " every man's death affected me , for i am involved in mankind , send not to ask for whom the bell tolls , it tolls for thee . "	說: 「 每個人的死亡都影響了我 , 我參與了曼金 , 寄來不要要求誰 , 讓鈴薯變得更好 。 」
for john donne , a recommendation of morality .	為約翰•唐尼 , 一個道德的建議 。
for us , i think , part of the equation for our survival .	對我們而言 , 我認為 , 我們生存的一部分 。
