they could define the viewing direction from which you want to generate an image for your visual imagery , so you can imagine what happened when you were at this wedding , for example .	他們可以定義你想要為你的視覺圖像產生一個圖像 , 所以你可以想像當你在這個婚禮時發生了什麼事 。
so this is just one example of a new era really in cognitive neuroscience where we're beginning to understand psychological processes like how you remember or imagine or even think in terms of the actions of the billions of individual neurons that make up our brains .	這只是一個新時代的一個例子 , 在認知神經科學中 , 我們開始了解心理過程 , 例如你如何記憶或想像或想像 , 甚至在數十億個個人神經元的行為中 , 構成我們的大腦 。
thank you very much .	非常感謝大家 。
imagine a global security driven by collaboration among agencies , government , the private sector and the public . that's not just the distant hope of opensource fans , it's the vision of james stavridis , the supreme commander of nato , who shares vivid moments from recent military history to explain why security of the future should be built with bridges rather than walls .	想像一個全球安全的驅動 , 由最近的軍隊、政府、私人部門和公共場所所所所合作 。 這不僅是開放法院的遠景 , 也是詹姆斯•史蒂迪的願景 , 俄羅斯的成功指揮者 , 他們分享了近期的軍事歷史 , 來解釋未來的安全性 , 而不是牆 。
collaboration , global issues , opensource , peace , politics , social media , violence , war	合作 , 全球議題、開放資源、和平、政治、社交媒體、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭 。
james stavridis: how nato's supreme commander thinks about global security	詹姆斯史蒂迪:娜托的最高指揮官想著全球安全性的問題 。
i'm gonna talk a little bit about opensource security , because we've got to get better at security in this 21st century .	我想要談談開放資源安全 , 因為我們必須在21世紀得到更好的安全 。
let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	首先 , 咱們回顧二十世紀 , 了解安全如何運作 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是verdun , 在法國的北方 , 一場戰鬥 , 只是在貝爾山的北部 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	1916年 , 超過30000年 , 七十萬人被殺 , 大約有兩千人一天 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果你把它推進第二次世界大戰中 , 你會看到史達丁丁的戰役 , 300天 , 兩百萬人死了 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 我們繼續嘗試建造牆 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從第一次世界大戰到第二次世界大戰 , 然後我們進入冷戰、鐵牆、柏林牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天的論點是 , 不是建立安全的牆 , 我們需要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲有名的橋 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它是德魯特河的橋樑 , 由伊凡•安德里的小說主題 , 談到歐洲和巴爾克人的一部分 , 隨著時間 , 已經有著巨大的牆壁 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	最近 , 在過去的十年 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 正開始 , 聚在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我再次爭論 , 開放資源安全是關聯國際、內部的介面 , 私人的共識 , 將它和策略溝通 , 大多在社交網路上 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球共同點在各種方式上 , 以威脅來源 , 沒有任何威脅來源 , 都會被建造牆上解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	很顯然 , 我是個帆船 。
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一條線 , 穿過印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片中有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	它在它的邊緣有環保電線 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	這就是防止海盜攻擊它 。
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	piracy今天是全世界非常活躍的威脅 。 這是印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	piracy也非常活躍在malacca的時代 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	在幾內亞灣 , 它是活躍的 。
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海看到它 。
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	這是全球運輸系統中的10億美金的距離 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 在那裡 , 有20艘船 , 500名火星人被告住 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是全球共同點的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要思考如何處理它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉換到不同類型的海 , 網路海 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這是兩個年輕人的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	那時 , 他們被監禁了 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們做了一份信用卡片 , 把它們連上一百億美金 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 它是全球經濟的2兆美金 。
two trillion a year .	每年有兩兆美元 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	這只是在英國的gdp下 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以這座網路海 , 我們無止境地是徹底的開放 , 也是威脅的 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	另一個我擔心全球共同點的威脅是被販賣、奈及利亞運動的威脅 , 來自歐洲的阿富汗 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心安東北的古柯鹼 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器和交易的動作 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人類販賣 , 以及它最糟糕的成本 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	販賣通常在海中移動 , 但在全球公有的其他部分 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你們 , 這是個非常高科技的我們用來阻止垃圾 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是用藥物卡爾的銷售 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	它在南美叢林裡建造 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那個低科技的雷射捕捉到 , 它帶著六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個 , 複雜的溝通 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	在人類、武器、上帝禁止 , 在大規模破壞的武器中 , 是全球公有威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	今天我們把它拉到阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是阿富汗的最快樂領域 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上有8%到90%的貧窮、鴉片和海洛因 , 來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	我們也看到恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是蓋達組織的位置 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個非常強烈的緊急機構 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義也是全球共同點的一部分 , 我們必須處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	這是21世紀 。
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道20世紀的工具不會成功 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我會爭論我們不會從槍枝的桶子裡傳遞安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會從槍枝的桶子裡傳送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這麼做時 , 我們一定要做得很好 , 競爭 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放資源安全是國際 , 介入 , 私人的聯繫 , 由網際網路上的策略溝通的想法 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這怎麼運作 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都在寫書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 那很奇怪 。 我覺得我讀過這個人口、年輕男性和女性 , 在二十歲和三十歲 , 大部分都是阿富汗的幻覺 。 」
you would be correct .	你是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全力量時 , 85%無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班在這些男人和女人學會閱讀時期的時期教育 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們閱讀文學課程 , 透過私人部門和開發機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教導了超過二十萬名阿富汗安全部隊去閱讀和寫基本層面 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你閱讀和寫在阿富汗時 , 你通常會把筆放在你的口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	當這些年輕人和女性畢業生時 , 他們把那筆筆錢放進口袋裡 , 把它放在口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這會帶來國際關係 , 全球有50個國家參與這個任務 , 這些發展機構 , 私人共和黨 , 以這種安全為基礎 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也教他們戰鬥技能 , 但我會爭論開放資源安全 , 意味著建立更久的安全效應 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國航海軍 。
it's called the comfort .	它叫做舒適 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一個姐妹船叫做 「 商業 」 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院船 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這首歌是舒適的 , 在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸 , 進行病人治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的危機上 , 他們會做四十萬個病人治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它不是由軍事而來的 , 而是藉由人道主義組織的組合:操作希望、專案微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織會發送志工 。
interagency physicians come out .	國際醫師出席了 。
they're all part of this .	他們都是這些 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子來說 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他媽媽一起走 , 兩天來到舒適的診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被吸引時 , 在他極端的眼睛中 , 他突然想到 , 說: 「 媽媽 , 維多多 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	多次以四十萬個病人治療 , 這種私人的共和黨合作 , 你開始看到創造安全的力量 , 以非常不同的方式創造安全 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你可以看到棒球員 。
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能否挑出這張照片中的兩個美國軍隊嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這些年輕男孩的兩位年輕男孩 。 這是一系列的棒球診所的一部分 , 在那裡 , 我們探討了主要的同事棒球 , 國家的部門 , 設立了這部電影 , 軍事棒球球球員 , 他們是真正的士兵 , 但參與這個任務 , 他們在拉丁美洲和加州的巴勒比亞 , 全國各地 , 全國各地 , 加州的巴勒比亞 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它給年輕男性和女性的角色 , 展現了社會的角色 , 以及我爭議的生命 , 協助為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這夥伴的另一面是災難的宗教 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍直升機在2004年被殺害了25萬人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些大災難中 , 2004年 , 25萬人死於巴基斯坦 , 2005年 , 8萬人死於海地地震 , 大約有30萬人死了 , 近期的地震組合 , 美國核能產業的核能產業 , 在這些領域中 , 我們看到了國際性行業的合作 , 和國際活動 , 和國際大自然的獨立 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些是開放資源安全的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它整合起來 , 越來越多 , 藉由這樣做 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你正在看這個想法: 「 啊 , 阿米蘭 , 這些必須是通訊的海道 , 或這些可能是纖維的電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 , 這是全球推特的圖表 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 。 綠色是地理 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是一個完美的演說 , 偉大的人口調查 , 世界上有六大的國家在描述秩序:中國、印度、facebook、twitter和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們要在這些蚊帳裡 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	為什麼我們要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們早就談到阿拉伯春天 , 所有這些力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉另一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表了一陣子的演講 。 我說 , 如同我對所有人說的 , 我在臉書上 , 朋友 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽眾聽起來有點笑 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章是由ap , 在電線上進行 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	在世界上兩個地方:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	頭條是:natoadto需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上 , 我有數百位臉書朋友 , 從印尼人和芬蘭說: 「 道德 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 喔 , 喔 , ~ 順便一提 , 娜托是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是的 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動訊息 , 移動訊息是我們如何聯繫國際 , 介入、私人的公共 , 這些社交網 , 協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我來打個十一月的音 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭警衛中 。
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在高爾蘭 , 在阿富汗南方 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡提醒我們 , 我不希望任何人離開房間思考 , 我們不需要有能力、競爭的軍隊才能創造真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這就是我們所做的核心 , 我們要保護自由、自由、言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍惜的事物 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道的 , 生命不是一場開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有一支軍事 , 不需要在艱難的戰鬥中或在巴拉克 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會爭論生命是旋轉的 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須把它放進去 , 如我在21世紀 , 我們要如何在真實戰爭和危機上創造安全性、私人的公共共共共通訊時 , 就會有時 , 但現在有許多例子 , 如同我們所說的 , 我們的軍隊可以創造21世紀的安全 , 國際安全、國際關係、私人的公共通訊 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我會說 , 我們今天早就聽到維基百科 。 我常常常用維基百科來看事實 , 儘管你們都很欣賞 , 維基百科不是由十二位聰明的人鎖在房間寫文章中 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天 , 數萬人輸入資訊 , 每一天 , 數百萬人都在做這些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	對於基本的點子來說 , 一個完美的圖像 , 沒有人像我們一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有人 , 沒有人盟友 , 沒有一個國家 , 我們沒有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的視覺表達非常簡單:每個人都能自由分享所有知識的總和 。
